O GILBY Improv'd;
Being a Correct Coppy of MR: O G ILBY'S
ACTUAL SURVEY ofallye Direct & Prin cipal Crofs
ROADS in ENGLAND and WALES:
Wherein are exactly Delineated & Engraven, Allye
CITIES, TOWNS, VILLAGES, CHURCHES, SEATS &C.
fcituate on or near the ROADS, with their refpective
Diftances in MEASURED and COMPUTED MILES.
And to renderthis-WORK universally Usefull & agreeable, [beyond
any of it's kind] are added in a clear & most Compendious Methods
1, A full & particular Defcription & Account of all the CITIES,
BOROUGH-TOWNS-CORPORATE &C.their ARMS,
Antiquity, Charters, Privilege, Trade, Rarities, &c. with-
fuitable Remarks on all Places of Note drawn from the beft HISTORIANS and ANTIQUARIES-
BY INO. O WEN of the MIDD: TEMPLE Gent.
2, The ARMS of the PEERS of this REALM whoderive
their Titles form Places lying on or near the ROADS
3, The ARMS of allye BISHOPRICKS & DEANARIES, their foun
-dation, Externt, Yearly- Calue, Number of Parithes &.c
4, The ARMS, & afuccinct Account of both UNIVERSTITIES
&theirrefpective COLLEGES, their foundations Fellowthips &.c
Laftly Particular & Correct MAPS-of allye Counties of SOUTHBRITAIN; nith a -
fummary description of each county, it's Circumference, Number of Acres, Boro & Market
Torvits Parishes, Air, Foil, Comodities, Manufaeture & [?]hat eack Pags in ye 2.th aid &,c
The Whate for its Compendious Variety & Exaetrifs, preferable to all BOOKS of
Roads hither to Pubtished or Proposed; and calculated not only for the direction of
the Traveller [as they are] but the general use of the Gentleman and Tradesmans
By EMAN: BOWEN Engraver -

A Table or Index of the Cities and Market Towns, &c. Thewing their Difiances from London,
and in what Page their respetive Roads are laid down .
The Numbers under C. are the computed Diftances, under M. F. the Meafure by Miles and
Furlongs, for Example, againft Barwick under C. M. F. you find 260. 339. 2 ; that is to
fay from London to Burdick is by Computation 260 Miles, by Meafure 339 Miles and 2
Furlongs, the Figure before the Line direfts you to Page 11, where you have the Road to
Berwick, and the Diftance of each Town, and fo of the reft.

A TABLE of the CITIES, TOWN, &c. defcribed in this Book.
THE EXPLANATION
TH E Title of every Road is a diftiftnft Page ;
to each of which is annexed a Map of the
County wherein the Initial or Boundary
City,Town, or PJace, lies [for the moft part] or elfe
fome part of the Defcription of the Road itfelf.
The beginning of the Road is always at the bot-
tom on the Left Hand, in the Page following the
Title j w hence you proceed upwards from i, 2,3,
4,5, &c. Miles until you come to the Top of the
ni ft Column, and fo on in like manner from the
Bottom of the 2d, &c, beginning in every
Page on the Left Hand as before directed.
The black Dots or Points in the middle of the
Road, aie the Stations of the Miles, with their
refpedlive numbers affixed to them.
When any other Road erodes or goes out of the
Road defcribed, there is an opening with the Name
of the Place to which it goes : And in your Progrefs
you meet with Rills, Brooks, Rivers, Bridges, [the
Pian of the Road /hewing whether built of Wood,
Brick, or Stone. Number of Arches contained in
eacn li any of Note.] Woods, Trees, Mountains,
and Hills [foewing their Afcent and Defcent, as
:hey really are, very naturally]. The Plan of the
Road foewing at the fame time the Ichnography of
all Cities, Towns, &c. and the Compafs in each
Column the true Bearings both of the Road itfelf
and of ail the Towns and Places that offer them-
felves to your View on either fide of it. The Road
I s . a ~k, e W a y bounded with two parallel black
Lines if inclofed or hedged in on both fades, or elfe
if open, with two parallel dotted Lines, or lafbly, if
bounded or hedged in on one fide and open on the other
with a black Line and a dotted Line parallel to it.
The Name of the County the Road paffes
through is engraved on each Column.
In the Margin or fome other convenient Place
°! ev " r y Pa 8 e 18 hkewife engraved a Defcription of
the Cities, Boroughs, [with the Arms of all f uc h
that have any] Corporations, Market Towns, and
whatever is remarkable, with figures referring to
the Places where they are to be found in the Plan
of that Road ; but to the Intent that the Reader
might readily find out any Place defcribed in this
Book, we have hereunto fubjoined an Alphabetical
Table oi all fuch Places. And whereas in the
whole courfe of thefe Roads there are manv Placet;
repeated often in the Plan : The Reader m„ft .W
fore have recourfe to the aforefaid Table, to dir eft
him to the Place he wants, it being defcribed only
m one. *
